 The fast of Utpana Ekadashi is a fast for healing, procreation and salvation
 mana jaataa he ki kisi bhi maansik samasya ho is vrath se dur ho jaati he
 This Ekadashi of Margashirsha Krishna Paksha is kept
 is baar utpanna ekadshi 03disambarako manaai jaaegi
 What are the rules to keep this fast? - This fast is kept in two ways - anhydrous fast and Falahari or aqueous fast
 - saamanytah nirjal vrath purna rup se swasthy vyakti ko hi rakhana chahie
 - Other or normal people should keep fasting or aquatic fast
 - is vrath main dashami ko ratri membhojananheen karnaa chahie
 - Shri Krishna is worshiped in the morning on Ekadashi
 - is vrath main keval falon kaa hi bhoga lagaaya jaataa he
 - It would be better to consume only water and fruits on this day
 kya karne se bachanaa chahie is din?- binabhagwan vishnuko arghya die hue din kii shuruyaat na karen

 6 years to this film that was all heart and changed my life! # raanjhanaa @sonamkapoor @dhanushkraja @aanandlrai @mohdzeeshanayyub # himanshusharma @cypplofficial @erosnowa post shared by Swara Bhasker (@reallyswara) on Jun 21, 2019 at 7:04 am pdtthese are stills from # raanjhanaa Of the # holi sequence that we filmed banaras in the freezing winter of mid-december 2012! Writer # himanshusharma had beautifully written a grand Holi sequence into the screenplay capturing the energy, scale, bhaang-induced madness of Banaras's traditional Holi
 It took us 3 days to shoot and the days chosen were 20, 21 and 22 December the COLDEST days of the year
 The art department had also constructed a keechad (mud / slush) pool, very thoughtfully filled with warm water which soon turned cold !!! There were almost 200 plus junior artists used for the scene, some of whom were pouring buckets of water from terraces on us while we ran through the streets
 i was scared of slipping and thus was barefoot!!! i have NEVER been so cold in my life as i was those three days
 But it was the MOST fun i've ever had shooting
 It was also the first time in my life that i played Holi in a sari
 
 The production was very sweet and kept blankets and buckets of hot water ready for us while we waited between shots
 Interestingly the writer Himanshu Sharma was missing during the filming of this sequence, he did not come on set as all the actors had sworn to throw him into the keechad pool for writing such a long and vast Holi sequence! :) # throwback # shootlife # raanjhanaamemories # 6yearsofraanjhanaaa post shared by Swara Bhasker (@reallyswara) on Jun 22, 2019 at 3:49 am PDT Actress Swara Bhaskar, who has always been active on social media, released her film 'raanjhanaa' (raanjhanaa) ) Has posted some pictures from her Instagram account on completion of 6 years

 Shatatila Ekadashi is celebrated on Krishna Paksha Ekadashi in Magh month
 is baar 31 janvari guuruuvaar ko shatatila ekadshi he
 Thursday and Ekadashi are considered to be the day of Lord Vishnu
 manyata he ki is din vishnu bhagwaan kaa paalan poshan karne se dhan laabh hota he
 On this day Krishna is also worshiped as an avatar of Vishnu
 ye bhi manyata he ki is din tilon kaa prayog karne se gyaan or dhan miltaa he
 It is said that Til is inhabited by Maha Lakshmi, so there is benefit in children's education, knowledge and wealth
 kaise karen shatatila ekadshi main til kaa prayog or puja-- kaale til or ganga jal daalkar snaan karen yaa munh dhoen
 If possible, observe Ekadashi fast
 - safed vastra dhaaran karen
 Worship Lord Vishnu and Krishna with fruit flowers and jaggery, sesame seeds
 - kaale til se havan karen
 - The mantra of worship will be chanting and Havan - Om Namo Bhagwate Vasudevaya - Chant this mantra 108 times
 - kaale til or gud kii mithai kaa prasad baante
 - Apply red vermilion tilak
 shatatila ekadshi kii katha-kaha jaataa he ki ek mahila bahut puja-paath, tapasya kiya karti thi
 The Lord became pleased with the woman and changed form, as a beggar, God asked for donations from that woman
 us mahila ne gusse main aakar bhagwaan ke paatr main ek pathar daal diya

 aise aalishaan makaan kaa mahila kya karti, jisamen khaane ko kuch bhi naa ho

 mana jaataa he ki prabhu ne us se kaha ki kathor tapasya karne ke baad jab tak kuch daan nahin karte hai, tab tak tapasya kaa puraa laabh nahin miltaa he
 Especially after fasting on Shatila Ekadashi, donate sesame and sesame sweets

 He asked his mps to take an aggressive stand against the bjp's attitude
 koyala block aavanton par niyantrak evam mahalekha pareekshak (sieji) kii report par sarkaar or congress donon hi vipakshi dal bhaajapa ke hamale jhel rahi hai
 Meanwhile, the Congress was attacked by its own ally, the Samajwadi Party (SP), saying that some Congress leaders might be willing to replace Manmohan Singh as the Prime Minister
 in sabake bich pradhanmantri manmohan singh iran kii yatra par ravaanaa ho gaye
 He gave his clarification on the issue in both houses of Parliament on Monday, rejecting bjp's demand for resignation
 sapa ke rajyasabha sadsy mohan singh ne kaha, "yah sambhav he ki congress ke kuch log manmohan singh kii jagah yuvaraj (rahul gandhi) ko laana chaahate hon
 Is this the internal trick of the Congress somewhere? " sonia ne sansadeey dal kii baithak main kaha ki yah 'sharmnaak or dukhad' he ki bhaajapa sansad kii kaarywahi chalane nahin de rahi he
 He also defended the demand for the resignation of Prime Minister Manmohan Singh by the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) on this issue as politically motivated
 sonia ne kaha, "bahes kaa uchit manch sansad hi he
 Blackmailing the Parliament as hostage has become the livelihood of the BJP
 yahaan tak ki iske kuch sahyogiyon ke liye bhi yah chintaa kaa kaaran he
 "he said that there is a lot to count the achievements of the public in the account of the UPA in the upcoming elections
 koyala block aavanton main motaa maal kamaane ke bhaajapa ke aaropon ko sire se khaarij karte hue sonia ne bhaajapa par jamkar palatwaar bhi kiye
 He said, "we will be more busy in elections in the coming days
" hamaare khate main bahut si uplabdhiyaan hai
 We have no need to be defensive
 ham apane samaksh maujuud chunautiyon se nipatane ko taiyaar hai
 We are not afraid of the opposition's allegations
 isliye hamen ladanaa he or ek uddeshy ke saath tathaa aakraamak hokar ladanaa he
 " congress adhyaksh ne kaha ki kaarywahi baadhit karnaa bhaajapa kaa rosemara kaa kaam ho gaya he
 "while serious issues are affecting the country, it is shameful and sad that the BJP is not allowing Parliament to function
" bhaajapa kaa yah ravaiya gaiyr-jimmedaarana he
 His attitude shows how much respect he has for democratic institutions
 unke bare main or kya kaha ja saktaa he jab unke varisht netaa hamaari sarkaar ko avaidh kehete hai or desh kii janata ne hamen jo janadesh diya he uskaa majaak udaate hai
 " gyaat ho ki bhaajapa netaa laalkrishna adwani ne pichley dinon sanyukt pragatisheel sarkaar kii vaidhata par sawaal uthaaya tha jiske baad sonia ne achaanak aakraamak rukh apana liya tha
 Later, Advani had to withdraw his statement
 sonia ne kaha, "maine pehle bhi kai baar kaha he or aage bhi kahuungi ki sarkaar or pradhanmantri kisi bhi mudde par charchaa ke liye hameshaa taiyaar hai
 The Prime Minister has given a clear, comprehensive and concrete statement in Parliament on coal allocation
 yah puri tarah se bhaajapa or uske dushprachaar kaa pole kholti he
 " blackmel karne ke sonia ke aarope kaa jawaab dete hue bhaajapa netaa arun jetali ne kaha, "ek sarkaar jisaki vishwaneeyata hi koyale ke saude main kaali ho gai he, use blackmel nahin kiya ja saktaa he
 " is bich, hangaame ke kaaran lagaataar chathe din sansad ke donon sadanon main kaarywahi baadhit hui
 After two adjournments in Lok Sabha and Rajya Sabha, the situation remained the same even when the proceedings started at 2 pm, after which the proceedings of both the Houses were adjourned for the whole day
 sansad kii kaarywahi isse pehle dopaher 12 baje tak or phir do baje tak ke liye sthagit kar di gai thi
 Although the BJP was not only involved in the uproar in both the houses of Parliament, but also the allies of the Dravida Munnetra Kazhagam (DMK), an ally of the United Progressive Alliance (UPA) government
 unka mudda haalanki bilkul alag tha
 The comments diemke ke saath-saath tamilnadu kii anya partiyon ne bhi srilanka ke sainikon ko prashikshan dene kaa virodh karte hue sansad main narebaaji kii or baad main sadan se bahirgaman kar gaye
 The BJP has been creating a ruckus in the Parliament since August 21 for its demand, due to which no parliamentary work is being done
 aise main aantarik suraksha, kisaanon, mahangaai tathaa aarthik susti se sambandhit vidheyakon kaa bhavishya adhar main latak gaya he
 Taking a dig at the BJP for constantly disrupting the proceedings of the Congress, Congress President Sonia Gandhi said in the party parliamentary party meeting that blackmail has become her livelihood
 unhone apane saansadon se bhaajapa ke ravaiye ke khilaaf aakraamak rukh akhriyaar karne ko kaha
 Both the government and the Congress are facing attacks from the opposition BJP on the Comptroller and Auditor General (CAG) report on coal block allocation
 is bich, congress par uske hi sahyogi samaajawaadee party (sapa) ne yah kehete hue hamalaa bolaa ki kuch congressi netaa shaayad pradhanmantri ke pad par manmohan singh kii jagah rahul gandhi ko laane ke icchhuk hai
 Amidst all this, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh left for a visit to Iran
 unhone istife kii bhaajapa kii maang ko khaarij karte hue somvaar ko sansad ke donon sadanon main is mudde par apni safai di thi
 SP Rajya Sabha member Mohan Singh said, "it is possible that some people of Congress want to replace Yuvraj (rahul Gandhi) in place of Manmohan Singh
 kahin yah congress kii aantarik chaal to nahin he!" Sonia said in a meeting of the parliamentary party that it is 'shameful and sad' that the BJP is not allowing Parliament to function
 is mudde par bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) dwaara kiye ja rahe pradhanmantri manmohan singh ke istife kii maang ko unhone raajnneeti se prerit bataakar unka bachaav bhi kiya
 Sonia said, "parliament is the appropriate forum for debate
 sansad ko bandhak banaakar blackmel karnaa hi bhaajapa kii roji-roti ban gai he
 Even for some of its associates, it is a cause for concern
 " unhone kaha ki aagaamee chunaavon main samprag ke khate main janata ko uplabdhiyaan ginane ko bahut kuch he
 Sonia also strongly attacked the BJP, dismissing the bjp's allegations of making big bucks in coal block allocation
 unhone kaha, "aane vaale dinon main ham chunaavon main zyada vyast rahenge
 There are many achievements in our account
 hamen rakshaatmak hone kii koi jarurat nahin he
 We are ready to meet the challenges before us
 ham vipaksh ke aaropon se ghabaraane vaale nahin he
 So we have to fight and fight with a purpose and aggressive
 " The Congress President said that it has become an everyday task for the BJP to disrupt the proceedings
 "aise main jabaki gambheer mudde desh ko prabhavit kar rahe hai, yah sharmnaak va dukhad he ki bhaajapa sansad kii kaarywahi nahin chalane de rahi he
 This attitude of the BJP is irresponsible
 uskaa ravaiya darshata he ki loktantric sansthaaon ke prati uske man main kitna sammaan he
 What else can be said about them when their senior leaders call our government illegal and the people of the country make fun of the mandate given to us
 " It may be known that BJP leader LK Advani had recently questioned the legitimacy of the United Progressive Government after which Sonia suddenly took an aggressive stance
 baad main adwani ko apana yah bayaan waapas lenaa padaa tha
 Sonia said, "I have said many times before and i will say that the government and the Prime Minister are always ready to discuss any issue
 pradhanmantri ne koyala aavanton par sansad main spasht, vyapak or thos bayaan diya he
 This completely exposes the BJP and its propaganda
 " Responding to Sonia's accusation of blackmailing, BJP leader Arun Jaitley said, "A government whose credibility has gone black in the coal deal cannot be blackmailed
" " Meanwhile, uproar disrupted proceedings in both houses of Parliament for the sixth consecutive day
 loksabhaa or rajyasabha main do baar ke sthagan ke baad dopaher do baje jab kaarywahi shuru hui tab bhi sthiti purvavat hi bani rahi, jiske baad donon sadanon kii kaarywahi puure din ke liye sthagit kar di gai
 Parliament proceedings were earlier adjourned till 12 noon and then till 2 pm
 sansad ke donon sadanon main hue hangaame main haalanki keval bhaajapa kii bhoomika nahin thi, balki sanyukt pragatisheel gathbandhan (samprag) sarkaar kii sahyogi dravid munetra kadgam (diemke) ke sahyogiyon ne bhi khub hangaamaa kiya
 Their issue however was completely different
 tippaniyan The DMK as well as other parties in Tamil Nadu also raised slogans in Parliament protesting the training of Sri Lankan soldiers and later walked out of the House
 bhaajapa apni maang ko lekar 21 agast se hi sansad main hangaamaa kar rahi he, jiske kaaran koi bhi sansadeey kaam nahin ho paa rahaa he
 In such a situation, the future of bills related to internal security, farmers, inflation and economic slowdown has been hanging in the balance

 Came across these pics of mine from school and college days

 Whn i look at these pics i feel proud of myself today not tht i felt any lesser abt myself back then
 Inspite of being so big i never let ppl's comments or ideas abt me bother me
 Bcoz it's my life and my body and only i hav the right to decide wht I'm gonna do with it
 Then one day i decided let me try how it feels to ba little lighter and hence started my weight loss journey
 It wasn't easy at all bt everytime i looked at the Progress in the mirror i got the push to do more
 i had lots more energy than before and i was loving every bit of this new person i was transforming into
 Whn i became a part of this industry, i had lost all my weight

 i continued on my fitness journey irrespective Bcoz fitness Fr me is a way of life now
